297→                sub->second->controlPlaneIdentifier());\n   298→    }\n   299→  }\n   300→\n   301→  pausable_ack_queue_.push(sub->second->handleResponse(response_proto));\n   302→ RS>::handleStreamEstablishmentFailure(\n   330→    bool next_attempt_may_send_initial_resource_version) {\n   331→  ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"GrpcMuxImpl stream failed to establish\");\n   332→  // If this happens while Envoy is still initializing, the onConfigUpdateFailed() we ultimately\n   333→  // call on CDS will cause LDS to start up, which adds to subscriptions_ here. So, to avoid a\n   334→  // crash, the iteration needs to dance around a little: collect pointers to all\n   335→  // SubscriptionStates, call on all those pointers we haven't yet called on, repeat if there are\n   336→  // now more SubscriptionStates.\n   337→  absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, S*> all_subscribed;\n   338→  absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, S*> already_called;\n   339→  do {\n   340→    for (auto& [type_url, subscription_state] : subscriptions_) {\n   341→      all_subscribed[type_url] = subscription_state.get();\n   342→    }\n   343→    for (auto& sub : all_subscribed) {\n   344→      if (already_called.insert(sub).second) { // insert succeeded ==> not already called\n   345→        sub.second->handleEstablishmentFailure();\n   346→      }\n   347→    }\n   348→  } while (all_subscribed.size() != subscriptions_.size());\n   349→  should_send_initial_resource_versions_ = next_attempt_may_send_initial_resource_version;\n   350→}\n   351→\n   352→template <class S, class F, class RQ, class RS>\n   353→S& GrpcMuxImpl<S, F, RQ, RS>::subscriptionStateFor(const std::string& type_url) {\n   354→  auto sub = subscriptions_.find(type_url);\n   355→  RELEASE_ASSERT(sub != {\n   372→  if (shutdown_) {\n   373→    return;\n   374→  }\n   375→\n   376→  while (true) {\n   377→    // Do any of our subscriptions even want to send a request?\n   378→    absl::optional<std::string> request_type_if_any = whoWantsToSendDiscoveryRequest();\n   379→    if (!request_type_if_any.has_value()) {\n   380→      break;\n   381→    }\n   382→    // If so, which one (by type_url)?\n   383→    std::string next_request_type_url = request_type_if_any.value();\n   384→    auto& sub = subscriptionStateFor(next_request_type_url);\n   385→    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"GrpcMuxImpl wants to send discovery request for {}\", next_request_type_url);\n   386→    // Try again later if paused/rate limited/stream down.\n   387→    if (!canSendDiscoveryRequest(next_request_type_url)) {\n   388→      break;\n   389→    }\n   390→    std::unique_ptr<RQ> request;\n   391→    // Get our subscription state to generate the appropriate discovery request, and send.\n   392→    if (!pausable_ack_queue_.empty()) {\n   393→      // Because ACKs take precedence over plain requests, if there is anything in the queue, it's\n   394→      // safe to assume it's of the type_url that we're wanting to send.\n   395→      //\n   396→      // getNextRequestWithAck() returns a raw unowned pointer, which sendGrpcMessage deletes.\n   397→      request = sub.getNextRequestWithAck(pausable_ack_queue_.popFront());\n   398→      ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"GrpcMuxImpl sent ACK discovery request for {}\", next_request_type_url);\n   399→    } else {\n   400→      // Returns a raw unowned pointer, which sendGrpcMessage deletes.\n   401→      request = sub.getNextRequestAckless();\n   402→      ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"GrpcMuxImpl sent non-ACK discovery request for {}\", next_request_type_url);\n   403→    }\n   404→    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"GrpcMuxImpl skip_subsequent_node: {}\", skipSubsequentNode());\n   405→    sendGrpcMessage(*request, sub);\n   406→  }\n   407→  maybeUpdateQueueSizeStat(pausable_ack_queue_.size());\n   408→}\n   409→\n   410→// Checks whether external conditions allow sending a discovery request. (Does not check\n   411→// whether we *want* to send a discovery request).\n   412→template <class S, class F, class RQ, class RS>\n   413→bool GrpcMuxImpl<S, F, RQ, RS>::canSendDiscoveryRequest(const std::string& type_url) {\n   414→  RELEASE_ASSERT(\n   415→      !pausable_ack_queue_.paused(type_url),\n   416→      fmt::format(\"canSendDiscoveryRequest() called on paused type_url {}. Pausedness is \"\n   417→                  \"supposed to be filtered out by whoWantsToSendDiscoveryRequest(). \",\n   418→                  type_url));\n   419→\n   420→  if (!grpcStreamAvailable()) {\n   421→    ENVOY_LOG(trace, \"No stream available to send a discovery request for {}.\", type_url);\n   422→    return false;\n   423→  } else if (!rateLimitAllowsDrain()) {\n   424→    ENVOY_LOG(trace, \"{} discovery request hit rate limit; will try later.\", type_url);\n   425→    return false;\n   426→  }\n   427→  return true;\n   428→}\n   429→\n   430→// Checks whether we have something to say in a discovery request, which can be an ACK and/or\n   431→// a subscription update. (Does not check whether we *can* send that discovery request).\n   432→// Returns the type_url we should send the discovery request for (if any).\n   433→// First, prioritizes ACKs over non-ACK subscription interest updates.\n   434→// Then, prioritizes non-ACK updates in the order the various types\n   435→// of subscriptions were activated.\n   436→template <class S, class F, class RQ, class RS>\n   437→absl::optional<std::string> GrpcMuxImpl<S, F, RQ, RS>::whoWantsToSendDiscoveryRequest() {\n   438→  // All ACKs are sent before plain updates. trySendDiscoveryRequests() relies on this. So, choose\n   439→  // type_url from pausable_ack_queue_ if possible, before looking at pending updates.\n   440→  if (!pausable_ack_queue_.empty()) {\n   441→    return pausable_ack_queue_.front().type_url_;\n   442→  }\n   443→  // If we're looking to send multiple non-ACK requests, send them in the order that their\n   444→  // subscriptions were initiated.\n   445→  for (const auto& sub_type : subscription_ordering_) {\n   446→    auto& sub = subscriptionStateFor(sub_type);\n   447→    if (sub.subscriptionUpdatePending() && !pausable_ack_queue_.paused(sub_type)) {\n   448→      return sub_type;\n   449→    }\n   450→  }\n   451→  return absl::nullopt;\n   452→}\n   453→\n   454→template class So, to avoid a\n  // crash, the iteration needs to dance around a little: collect pointers to all\n  // SubscriptionStates, call on all those pointers we haven't yet called on, repeat if there are\n  // now more SubscriptionStates.\n  absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, S*> all_subscribed;\n  absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, S*> already_called;\n  do {\n    for (auto& [type_url, subscription_state] : subscriptions_) {\n      all_subscribed[type_url] = subscription_state.get();\n    }\n    for (auto& sub : all_subscribed) {\n      if (already_called.insert(sub).second) { // insert succeeded ==> not already called\n        sub.second->handleEstablishmentFailure();\n      }\n    }\n  } while (all_subscribed.size() != subscriptions_.size());\n  should_send_initial_resource_versions_ = next_attempt_may_send_initial_resource_version;\n}\n\ntemplate <class S, class F, class RQ, class RS>\nS& GrpcMuxImpl<S, F, RQ, RS>::subscriptionStateFor(const std::string& type_url) {\n  auto sub =            type_url));\n  return *sub->second;\n}\n\ntemplate <class S, class F, class RQ, class RS>\nWatchMap& GrpcMuxImpl<S, F, RQ, RS>::watchMapFor(const std::string& type_url) {\n  auto watch_map // Do any of our subscriptions even want to send a request?\n    absl::optional<std::string> request_type_if_any = whoWantsToSendDiscoveryRequest();\n    if (!request_type_if_any.has_value()) {\n (Does not check whether we *can* send that discovery request).\n// Returns the type_url we should send the discovery request for (if any).\n// First, prioritizes ACKs over non-ACK subscription interest updates.\n// Then, prioritizes non-ACK updates in the order the various types\n// of subscriptions were activated.\ntemplate <class S, class F, class RQ, class RS>\nabsl::optional<std::string> GrpcMuxImpl<S, F, RQ, RS>::whoWantsToSendDiscoveryRequest() {\n  // All ACKs are sent before plain updates. trySendDiscoveryRequests() relies on this. xdstp://test/envoy.config.cluster.v3.Cluster/foo-cluster/*\n    40→// xdstp://test/envoy.config.cluster.v3.Cluster/foo-cluster/*?node.name=my_node\n    41→bool isXdsTpWildcard(const std::string& resource_name) {\n    42→  return XdsResourceIdentifier::hasXdsTpScheme(resource_name) &&\n    43→         (absl::EndsWith(resource_name, \"/*\") || absl::StrContains(resource_name, \"/*?\"));\n    44→}\n    45→\n    46→// Converts the XdsTp resource name to its wildcard equivalent.\n    47→// Must only be called on XdsTp resource names.\n    48→std::string convertToWildcard(const std::string& resource_name) {\n    49→  ASSERT(XdsResourceIdentifier::hasXdsTpScheme(resource_name));\n    50→  auto resource_or_error = XdsResourceIdentifier::decodeUrn(resource_name);\n    51→ 57→  options.sort_context_params_ = true;\n    58→  return XdsResourceIdentifier::encodeUrn(xdstp_resource, options);\n    59→}\n    60→} // namespace\n    61→\n 148→GrpcMuxImpl::~GrpcMuxImpl() { AllMuxes::get().erase(this); }\n   149→\n   150→void GrpcMuxImpl::shutdownAll() { AllMuxes::get().shutdownAll(); }\n   151→\n   152→void GrpcMuxImpl::onDynamicContextUpdate(absl::string_view resource_type_url) {\n   153→  auto api_state = api_state_.find(resource_type_url);\n   154→  if (api_state == api_state_.end()) {\n   155→ ASSERT(!started_);\n   163→  if (started_) {\n   164→    return;\n   165→  }\n   166→  started_ = true;\n   167→  grpc_stream_->establishNewStream();\n   168→}\n   169→\n   170→void GrpcMuxImpl::sendDiscoveryRequest(absl::string_view type_url) {\n   171→  if (shutdown_) {\n   172→    return;\n   173→  }\n   174→\n   175→  ApiState& api_state = apiStateFor(type_url);\n   176→  auto& request = api_state.request_;\n   177→  request.mutable_resource_names()->Clear();\n   178→\n   179→  // Maintain a set to avoid dupes.\n   180→  absl::node_hash_set<std::string> resources;\n   181→  for (const auto* watch : api_state.watches_) {\n   182→    for (const std::string& resource : watch->resources_) {\n   183→      if (!resources.contains(resource)) {\n   184→        resources.emplace(resource);\n   185→        request.add_resource_names(resource);\n   186→      }\n   187→    }\n   188→  }\n   189→\n   190→  if (api_state.must_send_node_ || !skip_subsequent_node_ || first_stream_request_) {\n   191→    // Node may have been cleared during a previous request.\n   192→    request.mutable_node()->CopyFrom(local_info_.node());\n   193→    api_state.must_send_node_ = false;\n   194→  } else {\n   195→    request.clear_node();\n   196→  }\n   197→  ENVOY_LOG(trace, \"Sending DiscoveryRequest for {}: {}\", type_url, request.ShortDebugString());\n   198→  grpc_stream_->sendMessage(request);\n   199→  first_stream_request_ = false;\n   200→\n   201→  // clear error_detail after the request is sent if it exists.\n   202→  if (apiStateFor(type_url).request_.has_error_detail()) {\n   203→    apiStateFor(type_url).request_.clear_error_detail();\n   204→  }\n   205→}\n   206→\n   207→void GrpcMuxImpl::clearNonce() {\n   208→  // Iterate over all api_states (for each type_url), and clear its nonce.\n   209→  for (auto& [type_url, api_state] : api_state_) {\n   210→    if (api_state) {\n   211→      api_state->request_.clear_response_nonce();\n   212→    }\n   213→  }\n   214→}\n   215→\n   216→void GrpcMuxImpl::loadConfigFromDelegate(const std::string& type_url,\n   217→                                         const absl::flat_hash_set<std::string>& resource_names) {\n   218→  if (!xds_resources_delegate_.has_value()) {\n   219→    return;\n   220→  }\n   221→  ApiState& api_state = apiStateFor(type_url);\n   222→  if (api_state.watches_.empty()) {\n   223→    // No watches, so exit without loading config from storage.\n   224→    return;\n   225→  }\n   226→\n   227→  const XdsConfigSourceId source_id{target_xds_authority_, type_url};\n   228→  TRY_ASSERT_MAIN_THREAD {\n   229→    std::vector<envoy::service::discovery::v3::Resource> resources =\n   230→        xds_resources_delegate_->getResources(source_id, resource_names);\n   231→    if (resources.empty()) {\n   232→      // There are no persisted resources, so nothing to process.\n   233→      return;\n   234→    }\n   235→\n   236→    std::vector<DecodedResourcePtr> decoded_resources;\n   237→    OpaqueResourceDecoder& resource_decoder = *api_state.watches_.front()->resource_decoder_;\n   238→    std::string version_info;\n   239→    for (const auto& resource : resources) {\n   240→      if (version_info.empty()) {\n   241→        version_info = resource.version();\n   242→      } else {\n   243→        ASSERT(resource.version() == version_info);\n   244→      }\n   245→\n   246→      TRY_ASSERT_MAIN_THREAD {\n   247→        decoded_resources.emplace_back(\n   248→            std::make_unique<DecodedResourceImpl>(resource_decoder, resource));\n   249→      }\n   250→      END_TRY\n   251→      CATCH(const EnvoyException& e,\n   252→            { xds_resources_delegate_->onResourceLoadFailed(source_id, resource.name(), e); });\n   253→    }\n   254→\n   255→    processDiscoveryResources(decoded_resources, api_state, type_url, version_info,\n   256→                              /*call_delegate=*/false);\n   257→  }\n   258→  END_TRY\n   259→  CATCH(const EnvoyException& e, {\n   260→    // TODO(abeyad): do something else here?\n   261→    ENVOY_LOG_MISC(warn, \"Failed to load config from delegate for {}: {}\", source_id.toKey(),\n   262→                   e.what());\n   263→  });\n   264→}\n   265→\n   266→GrpcMuxWatchPtr GrpcMuxImpl::addWatch(const std::string& type_url,\n   267→                                      const absl::flat_hash_set<std::string>& resources,\n   268→                                      SubscriptionCallbacks& callbacks,\n   269→                                      OpaqueResourceDecoderSharedPtr resource_decoder,\n   270→                                      const SubscriptionOptions& options) {\n   271→  // Resource cache is only used for EDS resources.\n   272→  EdsResourcesCacheOptRef resources_cache{absl::nullopt};\n   273→  if (eds_resources_cache_ &&\n   274→      (type_url == Config::getTypeUrl<envoy::config::endpoint::v3::ClusterLoadAssignment>())) {\n   275→    resources_cache = makeOptRefFromPtr(eds_resources_cache_.get());\n   276→  }\n   277→  auto watch = std::make_unique<GrpcMuxWatchImpl>(resources, callbacks, resource_decoder, type_url,\n   278→                                                  *this, options, local_info_, resources_cache);\n   279→  ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"gRPC mux addWatch for \" + type_url);\n   280→\n   281→  // Lazily kick off the requests based on first subscription. This has the\n   282→  // convenient side-effect that we order messages on the channel based on\n   283→  // Envoy's internal dependency ordering.\n   284→  // TODO(gsagula): move TokenBucketImpl params to a config.\n   285→  if (!apiStateFor(type_url).subscribed_) {\n   286→    apiStateFor(type_url).request_.set_type_url(type_url);\n   287→    apiStateFor(type_url).request_.mutable_node()->MergeFrom(local_info_.node());\n   288→    apiStateFor(type_url).subscribed_ = true;\n   289→    subscriptions_.emplace_back(type_url);\n   290→  }\n   291→\n   292→  // This will send an updated request on each subscription.\n   293→  // TODO(htuch): For RDS/EDS, this will generate a new DiscoveryRequest on each resource we added.\n   294→  // Consider in the future adding some kind of collation/batching during CDS/LDS updates so that we\n   295→  // only send a single RDS/EDS update after the CDS/LDS update.\n   296→  queueDiscoveryRequest(type_url);\n   297→\n   298→  return watch;\n   299→}\n   300→\n   301→absl::Status\n   302→GrpcMuxImpl::updateMuxSource(Grpc::RawAsyncClientSharedPtr&& primary_async_client,\n   303→                             Grpc::RawAsyncClientSharedPtr&& failover_async_client,\n   304→                             Stats::Scope& scope, BackOffStrategyPtr&& backoff_strategy,\n   305→                             const envoy::config::core::v3::ApiConfigSource& ads_config_source) {\n   306→  // Process the rate limit settings.\n   307→  absl::StatusOr<RateLimitSettings> rate_limit_settings_or_error =\n   308→      Utility::parseRateLimitSettings(ads_config_source);\n   309→  RETURN_IF_NOT_OK_REF(rate_limit_settings_or_error.status());\n   310→\n   311→  const Protobuf::MethodDescriptor& service_method =\n   312→      *Protobuf::DescriptorPool::generated_pool()->FindMethodByName(\n   313→          \"envoy.service.discovery.v3.AggregatedDiscoveryService.StreamAggregatedResources\");\n   314→\n   315→  // Disconnect from current xDS servers.\n   316→  ENVOY_LOG_MISC(info, \"Replacing xDS gRPC mux source\");\n   317→  grpc_stream_->closeStream();\n   318→  grpc_stream_ = createGrpcStreamObject(std::move(primary_async_client),\n   319→                                        std::move(failover_async_client), service_method, scope,\n   320→                                        std::move(backoff_strategy), *rate_limit_settings_or_error);\n   321→  // No need to update the config_validators_ as they may contain some state\n   322→  // that needs to be kept across different GrpcMux objects.\n   323→\n   324→  // Start the subscriptions over the grpc_stream.\n   325→  grpc_stream_->establishNewStream();\n   326→\n   327→  return absl::OkStatus();\n   328→}\n   329→\n   330→ScopedResume GrpcMuxImpl::pause(const std::string& type_url) {\n   331→  return pause(std::vector<std::string>{type_url});\n   332→}\n   333→\n   334→ScopedResume GrpcMuxImpl::pause(const std::vector<std::string> type_urls) {\n   335→  for (const auto& type_url : type_urls) {\n   336→    ApiState& api_state = apiStateFor(type_url);\n   337→    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"Pausing discovery requests for {} (previous count {})\", type_url,\n   338→              api_state.pauses_);\n   339→    ++api_state.pauses_;\n   340→  }\n   341→  return std::make_unique<Cleanup>([this, type_urls]() {\n   342→    for (const auto& type_url : type_urls) {\n   343→      ApiState& api_state = apiStateFor(type_url);\n   344→      ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"Decreasing pause count on discovery requests for {} (previous count {})\",\n   345→                type_url, api_state.pauses_);\n   346→      ASSERT(api_state.paused());\n   347→\n   348→      if (--api_state.pauses_ == 0 && api_state.pending_ && api_state.subscribed_) {\n   349→        ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"Resuming discovery requests for {}\", type_url);\n   350→        queueDiscoveryRequest(type_url);\n   351→        api_state.pending_ = false;\n   352→      }\n   353→    }\n   354→  });\n   355→}\n   356→\n   357→void GrpcMuxImpl::onDiscoveryResponse(\n   358→    std::unique_ptr<envoy::service::discovery::v3::DiscoveryResponse>&& message,\n   359→    ControlPlaneStats& control_plane_stats) {\n   360→  const std::string type_url = message->type_url();\n   361→  ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"Received gRPC message for {} at version {}\", type_url, message->version_info());\n   362→\n   363→  if (api_state_.count(type_url) == 0) {\n   364→    // TODO(yuval-k): This should never happen. consider dropping the stream as this is a\n   365→    // protocol violation\n   366→    ENVOY_LOG(warn, \"Ignoring the message for type URL {} as it has no current subscribers.\",\n   367→              type_url);\n   368→    return;\n   369→  }\n   370→\n   371→  ApiState& api_state = apiStateFor(type_url);\n   372→\n   373→  if (message->has_control_plane()) {\n   374→    control_plane_stats.identifier_.set(message->control_plane().identifier());\n   375→\n   376→    if (message->control_plane().identifier() != api_state.control_plane_identifier_) {\n   377→      api_state.control_plane_identifier_ = message->control_plane().identifier();\n   378→      ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"Receiving gRPC updates for {} from {}\", type_url,\n   379→                api_state.control_plane_identifier_);\n   380→    }\n   381→  }\n   382→\n   383→  if (api_state.watches_.empty()) {\n   384→    // update the nonce as we are processing this response.\n   385→    api_state.request_.set_response_nonce(message->nonce());\n   386→    if (message->resources().empty()) {\n   387→      // No watches and no resources. This can happen when envoy unregisters from a\n   388→      // resource that's removed from the server as well. For example, a deleted cluster\n   389→      // triggers un-watching the ClusterLoadAssignment watch, and at the same time the\n   390→      // xDS server sends an empty list of ClusterLoadAssignment resources. we'll accept\n   391→      // this update. no need to send a discovery request, as we don't watch for anything.\n   392→      api_state.request_.set_version_info(message->version_info());\n   393→    } else {\n   394→      // No watches and we have resources - this should not happen. send a NACK (by not\n   395→      // updating the version).\n   396→      ENVOY_LOG(warn, \"Ignoring unwatched type URL {}\", type_url);\n   397→      queueDiscoveryRequest(type_url);\n   398→    }\n   399→    return;\n   400→  }\n   401→  ScopedResume same_type_resume;\n   402→  // We pause updates of the same type. This is necessary for SotW and GrpcMuxImpl, since unlike\n   403→  // delta and NewGRpcMuxImpl, independent watch additions/removals trigger updates regardless of\n   404→  // the delta state. The proper fix for this is to converge these implementations,\n   405→  // see https://github.com/envoyproxy/envoy/issues/11477.\n   406→  same_type_resume = pause(type_url);\n   407→  TRY_ASSERT_MAIN_THREAD {\n   408→    std::vector<DecodedResourcePtr> resources;\n   409→    OpaqueResourceDecoder& resource_decoder = *api_state.watches_.front()->resource_decoder_;\n   410→\n   411→    for (const auto& resource : message->resources()) {\n   412→      // TODO(snowp): Check the underlying type when the resource is a Resource.\n   413→      if (!resource.Is<envoy::service::discovery::v3::Resource>() &&\n   414→          type_url != resource.type_url()) {\n   415→        throwEnvoyExceptionOrPanic(\n   416→            fmt::format(\"{} does not match the message-wide type URL {} in DiscoveryResponse {}\",\n   417→                        resource.type_url(), type_url, message->DebugString()));\n   418→      }\n   419→\n   420→      auto decoded_resource = THROW_OR_RETURN_VALUE(\n   421→          DecodedResourceImpl::fromResource(resource_decoder, resource, message->version_info()),\n   422→          DecodedResourceImplPtr);\n   423→\n   424→      if (!isHeartbeatResource(type_url, *decoded_resource)) {\n   425→        resources.emplace_back(std::move(decoded_resource));\n   426→      }\n   427→    }\n   428→\n   429→    processDiscoveryResources(resources, api_state, type_url, message->version_info(),\n   430→                              /*call_delegate=*/true);\n   431→\n   432→    // Processing point when resources are successfully ingested.\n   433→    if (xds_config_tracker_.has_value()) {\n   434→      xds_config_tracker_->onConfigAccepted(type_url, resources);\n   435→    }\n   436→  }\n   437→  END_TRY\n   438→  CATCH(const EnvoyException& e, {\n   439→    for (auto watch : api_state.watches_) {\n   440→      watch->callbacks_.onConfigUpdateFailed(\n   441→          Envoy::Config::ConfigUpdateFailureReason::UpdateRejected, &e);\n   442→    }\n   443→    ::google::rpc::Status* error_detail = api_state.request_.mutable_error_detail();\n   444→    error_detail->set_code(Grpc::Status::WellKnownGrpcStatus::Internal);\n   445→    error_detail->set_message(Config::Utility::truncateGrpcStatusMessage(e.what()));\n   446→\n   447→    // Processing point when there is any exception during the parse and ingestion process.\n   448→    if (xds_config_tracker_.has_value()) {\n   449→      xds_config_tracker_->onConfigRejected(*message, error_detail->message());\n   450→    }\n   451→  });\n   452→  api_state.previously_fetched_data_ = true;\n   453→  api_state.request_.set_response_nonce(message->nonce());\n   454→  ASSERT(api_state.paused());\n   455→  queueDiscoveryRequest(type_url);\n   456→}\n   457→\n   458→void GrpcMuxImpl::processDiscoveryResources(const std::vector<DecodedResourcePtr>& resources,\n   459→                                            ApiState& api_state, const std::string& type_url,\n   460→                                            const std::string& version_info,\n   461→                                            const bool call_delegate) {\n   462→  ASSERT_IS_MAIN_OR_TEST_THREAD();\n   463→  // To avoid O(n^2) explosion (e.g. when we have 1000s of EDS watches), we\n   464→  // build a map here from resource name to resource and then walk watches_.\n   465→  // We have to walk all watches (and need an efficient map as a result) to\n   466→  // ensure we deliver empty config updates when a resource is dropped. We make the map ordered\n   467→  // for test determinism.\n   468→  absl::btree_map<std::string, DecodedResourceRef> resource_ref_map;\n   469→  std::vector<DecodedResourceRef> all_resource_refs;\n   470→\n   471→  const auto scoped_ttl_update = api_state.ttl_.scopedTtlUpdate();\n   472→\n   473→  for (const auto& resource : resources) {\n   474→    if (resource->ttl()) {\n   475→      api_state.ttl_.add(*resource->ttl(), resource->name());\n   476→    } else {\n   477→      api_state.ttl_.clear(resource->name());\n   478→    }\n   479→\n   480→    all_resource_refs.emplace_back(*resource);\n   481→    if (XdsResourceIdentifier::hasXdsTpScheme(resource->name())) {\n   482→      // Sort the context params of an xdstp resource, so we can compare them easily.\n   483→      auto resource_or_error = XdsResourceIdentifier::decodeUrn(resource->name());\n   484→      THROW_IF_NOT_OK_REF(resource_or_error.status());\n   485→      xds::core::v3::ResourceName xdstp_resource = resource_or_error.value();\n   486→      XdsResourceIdentifier::EncodeOptions options;\n   487→      options.sort_context_params_ = true;\n   488→      resource_ref_map.emplace(XdsResourceIdentifier::encodeUrn(xdstp_resource, options),\n   489→                               *resource);\n   490→    } else {\n   491→      resource_ref_map.emplace(resource->name(), *resource);\n   492→    }\n   493→  }\n   494→\n   495→  // Execute external config validators if there are any watches.\n   496→  if (!api_state.watches_.empty()) {\n   497→    config_validators_->executeValidators(type_url, resources);\n   498→  }\n   499→\n   500→  for (auto watch : api_state.watches_) {\n   501→    // onConfigUpdate should be called in all cases for single watch xDS (Cluster and\n   502→    // Listener) even if the message does not have resources so that update_empty stat\n   503→    // is properly version_info));\n   506→      continue;\n   507→    }\n   508→    std::vector<DecodedResourceRef> found_resources;\n   509→    for (const auto& watched_resource_name : watch->resources_) {\n   510→      // Look for a singleton subscription.\n   511→      auto it = resource_ref_map.find(watched_resource_name);\n   512→      if (it != resource_ref_map.end()) {\n   513→        found_resources.emplace_back(it->second);\n   514→      } else if (isXdsTpWildcard(watched_resource_name)) {\n   515→        // See if the resources match the xdstp wildcard subscription.\n   516→        // Note: although it is unlikely that Envoy will need to support a resource that is mapped\n   517→        // to both a singleton and collection watch, this code still supports this use case.\n   518→        // TODO(abeyad): This could be made more efficient, e.g. by pre-computing and having a map\n   519→        // entry for each wildcard watch.\n   520→        for (const auto& resource_ref_it : resource_ref_map) {\n   521→          if (XdsResourceIdentifier::hasXdsTpScheme(resource_ref_it.first) &&\n   522→              convertToWildcard(resource_ref_it.first) == watched_resource_name) {\n   523→            found_resources.emplace_back(resource_ref_it.second);\n   524→          }\n   525→        }\n   526→      }\n   527→    }\n   528→\n   529→    // onConfigUpdate should be called only on watches(clusters/listeners) that have\n   530→    // updates in the message for EDS/RDS.\n   531→    if (!found_resources.empty()) {\n   532→      THROW_IF_NOT_OK(watch->callbacks_.onConfigUpdate(found_resources, version_info));\n   533→      // Resource cache is only used for EDS resources.\n   534→      if (eds_resources_cache_ &&\n   535→          (type_url == Config::getTypeUrl<envoy::config::endpoint::v3::ClusterLoadAssignment>())) {\n   536→        for (const auto& resource : found_resources) {\n   537→          const 546→    }\n   547→  }\n   548→\n   549→  // All config updates have been applied without throwing an exception, so we'll call the xDS\n   550→  // resources delegate, if any.\n   551→  if               all_resource_refs);\n   554→  }\n   555→\n   556→  // TODO(mattklein123): In the future if we start tracking per-resource versions, we\n   557→  // would do that tracking here.\n   558→ *Protobuf::DescriptorPool::generated_pool()->FindMethodByName(\n          \"envoy.service.discovery.v3.AggregatedDiscoveryService.StreamAggregatedResources\");\n\n  // Disconnect from current xDS servers.\n  ENVOY_LOG_MISC(info, \"Replacing xDS gRPC mux source\");\n  grpc_stream_->closeStream();\n  grpc_stream_ = createGrpcStreamObject(std::move(primary_async_client),\n                                        std::move(failover_async_client), service_method, scope,\n                                        std::move(backoff_strategy), *rate_limit_settings_or_error);\n  // No need to update pause(std::vector<std::string>{type_url});\n}\n\nScopedResume GrpcMuxImpl::pause(const std::vector<std::string> type_urls) {\n  for (const auto& type_url : type_urls) {\n    ApiState& api_state = apiStateFor(type_url);\n    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"Pausing discovery requests for {} (previous count {})\", type_url,\n              api_state.pauses_);\n    ++api_state.pauses_;\n  }\n  return std::make_unique<Cleanup>([this, type_urls]() {\n    for (const auto& type_url : type_urls) {\n      ApiState& api_state = apiStateFor(type_url);\n      ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"Decreasing pause count on discovery requests for {} (previous count {})\",\n                type_url, api_state.pauses_);\n      ASSERT(api_state.paused());\n\n      if (--api_state.pauses_ == 0 && api_state.pending_ && api_state.subscribed_) {\n        ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"Resuming discovery requests for {}\", type_url);\n        queueDiscoveryRequest(type_url);\n        api_state.pending_ = false;\n      }\n    }\n type_url = message->type_url();\n  ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"Received gRPC message for {} at version {}\", type_url, message->version_info());\n\n  if (api_state_.count(type_url) == 0) {\n    // TODO(yuval-k): This should never happen. consider dropping the stream as this is a\n    // protocol violation\n    ENVOY_LOG(warn, \"Ignoring the message for type URL {} as it has no current subscribers.\",\n              type_url);\n    return;\n  }\n\n  ApiState& api_state = apiStateFor(type_url);\n\n  if (message->has_control_plane()) {\n    control_plane_stats.identifier_.set(message->control_plane().identifier());\n\n    if (message->control_plane().identifier() != api_state.control_plane_identifier_) {\n      api_state.control_plane_identifier_ = message->control_plane().identifier();\n      ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"Receiving gRPC updates for {} from {}\", type_url,\n                api_state.control_plane_identifier_);\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (api_state.watches_.empty()) {\n    // update the nonce as we are processing this response.\n    api_state.request_.set_response_nonce(message->nonce());\n    if (message->resources().empty()) {\n      // No watches and no resources. This can happen when envoy unregisters from a\n      // resource that's removed from the server as well. For example, a deleted cluster\n      // triggers un-watching the ClusterLoadAssignment watch, and at the same time the\n      // xDS server sends an empty list of ClusterLoadAssignment resources. we'll accept\n      // this update. no need to send a discovery request, as we don't watch for anything.\n      api_state.request_.set_version_info(message->version_info());\n    } else {\n      // No watches and we have resources - this should not happen. send a NACK (by not\n      // updating the version).\n      ENVOY_LOG(warn, \"Ignoring unwatched type URL {}\", type_url);\n      queueDiscoveryRequest(type_url);\n    }\n    return;\n  }\n  ScopedResume same_type_resume;\n  // We pause updates of the same type. This is necessary for SotW and GrpcMuxImpl, since unlike\n  // delta and NewGRpcMuxImpl, independent watch additions/removals trigger updates regardless of\n  // the delta state. The proper fix for this is to converge these implementations,\n  // see https://github.com/envoyproxy/envoy/issues/11477.\n  same_type_resume = pause(type_url);\n  TRY_ASSERT_MAIN_THREAD {\n    std::vector<DecodedResourcePtr> resources;\n    OpaqueResourceDecoder& resource_decoder = *api_state.watches_.front()->resource_decoder_;\n\n    for (const auto& resource : message->resources()) {\n      // TODO(snowp): Check the underlying type when the resource is a Resource.\n      if (!resource.Is<envoy::service::discovery::v3::Resource>() &&\n          type_url != resource.type_url()) {\n        throwEnvoyExceptionOrPanic(\n            fmt::format(\"{} does not match the message-wide type URL {} in DiscoveryResponse {}\",\n                        resource.type_url(), type_url, message->DebugString()));\n      }\n\n      auto decoded_resource = THROW_OR_RETURN_VALUE(\n          DecodedResourceImpl::fromResource(resource_decoder, resource, message->version_info()),\n          DecodedResourceImplPtr);\n\n      if (!isHeartbeatResource(type_url, *decoded_resource)) {\n        resources.emplace_back(std::move(decoded_resource));\n      }\n    }\n\n    processDiscoveryResources(resources, api_state, type_url, message->version_info(),\n                              /*call_delegate=*/true);\n\n    // Processing point when resources are successfully ingested.\n    if (xds_config_tracker_.has_value()) {\n      xds_config_tracker_->onConfigAccepted(type_url, resources);\n    }\n  }\n  END_TRY\n  CATCH(const EnvoyException& e, {\n    for (auto watch : api_state.watches_) {\n      watch->callbacks_.onConfigUpdateFailed(\n          Envoy::Config::ConfigUpdateFailureReason::UpdateRejected, &e);\n    }\n    ::google::rpc::Status* error_detail = api_state.request_.mutable_error_detail();\n    error_detail->set_code(Grpc::Status::WellKnownGrpcStatus::Internal);\n    error_detail->set_message(Config::Utility::truncateGrpcStatusMessage(e.what()));\n\n    // Processing point when there is any exception during the parse and ingestion process.\n    if (xds_config_tracker_.has_value()) {\n      xds_config_tracker_->onConfigRejected(*message, error_detail->message());\n    }\n  });\n  api_state.previously_fetched_data_ = true;\n  api_state.request_.set_response_nonce(message->nonce());\n  ASSERT(api_state.paused());\n  queueDiscoveryRequest(type_url);\n}\n\nvoid GrpcMuxImpl::processDiscoveryResources(const std::vector<DecodedResourcePtr>& resources,\n                                            ApiState& api_state, const std::string& type_url,\n                                            const std::string& version_info,\n                                            const bool call_delegate) {\n  ASSERT_IS_MAIN_OR_TEST_THREAD();\n  // To avoid O(n^2) explosion (e.g. when we have 1000s of EDS watches), we\n  // build a map here from resource name to resource and then walk watches_.\n  // We have to walk all watches (and need an efficient map as a result) to\n  // ensure we deliver empty config updates when a resource is dropped. We make the map ordered\n  // for test determinism.\n  absl::btree_map<std::string, DecodedResourceRef> resource_ref_map;\n  std::vector<DecodedResourceRef> all_resource_refs;\n\n  const auto scoped_ttl_update = api_state.ttl_.scopedTtlUpdate();\n\n  for (const auto& resource : resources) {\n    if (resource->ttl()) {\n      api_state.ttl_.add(*resource->ttl(), resource->name());\n    } else {\n      api_state.ttl_.clear(resource->name());\n    }\n\n    all_resource_refs.emplace_back(*resource);\n    if (XdsResourceIdentifier::hasXdsTpScheme(resource->name())) {\n      // Sort the context params of an xdstp resource, so we can compare them easily.\n      auto resource_or_error = XdsResourceIdentifier::decodeUrn(resource->name());\n      THROW_IF_NOT_OK_REF(resource_or_error.status());\n      xds::core::v3::ResourceName xdstp_resource = resource_or_error.value();\n      XdsResourceIdentifier::EncodeOptions options;\n      options.sort_context_params_ = true;\n      resource_ref_map.emplace(XdsResourceIdentifier::encodeUrn(xdstp_resource, options),\n                               *resource);\n    } else {\n      resource_ref_map.emplace(resource->name(), *resource);\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Execute external config validators if there are any watches.\n  if (!api_state.watches_.empty()) {\n    config_validators_->executeValidators(type_url, resources);\n  }\n\n  for (auto watch : api_state.watches_) {\n    // onConfigUpdate should be called in all cases for single watch xDS (Cluster and\n    // Listener) even if the message does not have resources so that update_empty stat\n    // is properly incremented and state-of-the-world semantics are maintained.\n    if (watch->resources_.empty()) {\n      THROW_IF_NOT_OK(watch->callbacks_.onConfigUpdate(all_resource_refs, version_info));\n      continue;\n    }\n    std::vector<DecodedResourceRef> found_resources;\n    for (const auto& watched_resource_name : watch->resources_) {\n      // Look for a singleton subscription.\n      auto it = resource_ref_map.find(watched_resource_name);\n      if (it != resource_ref_map.end()) {\n        found_resources.emplace_back(it->second);\n      } else if (isXdsTpWildcard(watched_resource_name)) {\n        // See if the resources match the xdstp wildcard subscription.\n        // Note: although it is unlikely that Envoy will need to support a resource that is mapped\n        // to both a singleton and collection watch, this code still supports this use case.\n        // TODO(abeyad): This could be made more efficient, e.g. by pre-computing and having a map\n        // entry for each wildcard watch.\n        for (const auto& resource_ref_it : resource_ref_map) {\n          if (XdsResourceIdentifier::hasXdsTpScheme(resource_ref_it.first) &&\n              convertToWildcard(resource_ref_it.first) == watched_resource_name) {\n            found_resources.emplace_back(resource_ref_it.second);\n          }\n        }\n      }\n    }\n\n    // onConfigUpdate should be called only on watches(clusters/listeners) that have\n    // updates in the message for EDS/RDS.\n    if (!found_resources.empty()) {\n      THROW_IF_NOT_OK(watch->callbacks_.onConfigUpdate(found_resources, version_info));\n      // Resource cache is only used for EDS resources.\n      if (eds_resources_cache_ &&\n          (type_url == Config::getTypeUrl<envoy::config::endpoint::v3::ClusterLoadAssignment>())) {\n        for (const auto& resource : found_resources) {\n          const envoy::config::endpoint::v3::ClusterLoadAssignment& cluster_load_assignment =\n              dynamic_cast<const envoy::config::endpoint::v3::ClusterLoadAssignment&>(\n                  resource.get().resource());\n          eds_resources_cache_->setResource(resource.get().name(), cluster_load_assignment);\n        }\n        // No need to remove resources from the cache, as currently only non-collection\n        // subscriptions are supported, and these resources are removed in the call\n        // to updateWatchInterest().\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  // All config updates have been applied without throwing an exception, so we'll call the xDS\n  // resources delegate, if any.\n  if (call_delegate && xds_resources_delegate_.has_value()) {\n    xds_resources_delegate_->onConfigUpdated(XdsConfigSourceId{target_xds_authority_, type_url},\n                                             all_resource_refs);\n  }\n\n  // TODO(mattklein123): In the future if we start tracking per-resource versions, we\n  // would do that tracking here.\n  api_state.request_.set_version_info(version_info);\n  Memory::Utils::tryShrinkHeap();\n}\n\nvoid GrpcMuxImpl::onWriteable() { drainRequests(); }\n\nvoid GrpcMuxImpl::onStreamEstablished() {\n  first_stream_request_ = true;\n  grpc_stream_->maybeUpdateQueueSizeStat(0);\n  clearNonce();\n limiting is not enabled at all or if it is under rate limit.\n    sendDiscoveryRequest(request_queue_->front());\n    request_queue_->pop();\n  }\n
